      </td>
      <td valign="middle" class="td2">
        <p class="p2"><span class="s1">&lt;p class="lede"&gt;High-rises, high prices, and high blood pressures are common in NYC’s famous Financial District. This financial epicenter's looming buildings bankroll it as one of the city's most recognizable neighborhoods. Financial District may rush by at lightning-speed during the day, but once the last fast-talking mogul leaves for the evening this neighborhood quickly quiets down.&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
